  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不平衡最优传输方法将细胞群体视为连续流体，在宏观层面推断轨迹，但无法捕捉单细胞分辨率下离散的、跳跃式的分裂-死亡事件，而这些事件对理解谱系分支和细胞命运决定至关重要。本文旨在开发一个能同时处理随机效应和非平衡质量动力学、并在单细胞层面模拟离散事件的框架。

Method: 提出Unbalanced Schrödinger Bridge (USB)框架，通过求解Branching Schrödinger Bridge (BSB)问题，为每个细胞建立微观动力学模型：同时进行布朗运动和离散的分裂-死亡跳跃。方法采用无需模拟的训练目标，通过高效求解器实现高维组学数据的可扩展性，避免了传统模拟的计算负担。

Result: 在模拟和真实数据集上验证表明：1) USB的轨迹重建性能优于或等同于确定性基线方法；2) 首次实现单细胞分辨率下真实的分裂-死亡动力学离散模拟，这是现有方法无法完成的关键突破。

Conclusion: USB框架提供了理论严谨且计算高效的解决方案，成功桥接了群体连续模型与单细胞离散动力学的鸿沟。该方法不仅提升了轨迹推断精度，更重要的是解锁了单细胞层面离散分裂-死亡事件模拟的新能力，为研究细胞命运决定机制提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Inferring cellular trajectories from destructive snapshots is complicated by the challenges of stochasticity and non-conservative mass dynamics such as cell proliferation and apoptosis. Existing unbalanced Optimal Transport (OT) methods treat mass as a continuous fluid, performing inference at the population level. However, this macroscopic view often fails to capture the discrete, jump-like nature of birth-death events at single-cell resolution, which is essential for understanding lineage branching and fate decisions. We present Unbalanced Schrödinger Bridge (USB), a simulation-free framework for learning underlying dynamics that effectively integrates both stochastic and unbalanced effects which also models the discrete, jump-like birth-death dynamics at single-cell resolution. Theoretically, USB provides a tractable solution to the Branching Schrödinger Bridge (BSB) problem, offering a rigorous microscopic interpretation where individual cells undergo both Brownian motion and discrete birth-death jumps. Technically, the method implements an efficient solver by introducing a simulation-free training objective that effectively scales to high-dimensional omics data. Empirically, we demonstrate on both simulated and real-world datasets that USB not only achieves trajectory reconstruction performance better than or comparable to deterministic baselines but also uniquely enables realistic discrete simulation of birth-death dynamics at single-cell resolution.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出GD4方法，采用图基离散去噪扩散框架，直接在离散符号空间中操作（而非连续松弛空间），支持一次或少数几次去噪评估即可实现快速推理。

Abstract: In wireless communications, recovering the optimal solution to the multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO) detection problem is NP-hard. Obtaining high-quality suboptimal solutions with a favorable performance-complexity trade-off is particularly challenging in under-determined systems with $N_t$ transmit antennas and $N_r < N_t$ receive antennas. Recent diffusion-based MIMO detectors have shown promise, but they require extensive sampling iterations at inference time, and their performance degrades in under-determined scenarios. We propose GD4, a graph-based discrete denoising diffusion method for MIMO detection. Unlike existing diffusion-based detectors that operate in a continuous relaxed space, GD4 performs denoising directly in the discrete symbol space and enables fast inference with one or a few denoising evaluations. Numerical results show that, under a similar inference-time compute budget, GD4 produces higher-quality suboptimal solutions than existing diffusion-based detectors and some widely used classical baseline including box-constrained Babai point and the $K$-best box-constrained randomized Klein-Babai point in both under-determined and overdetermined settings.

Result: 在2016--2026年AMD、黄金、GBP/USD等波动金融数据集的广泛基准测试中，SA-BCP在不同置信水平下持续最小化严格适当的Winkler评分。具体而言，它消除了ACI变体的系统性欠覆盖，并在高置信度请求下将贝叶斯CP的区间膨胀降低了10\%至37\%。

Conclusion: SA-BCP通过优雅地导航偏差-方差权衡，在条件可靠性与预测效率之间实现了最优平衡，为波动环境下的在线预测提供了理论保障和实践优势。

Abstract: Online Conformal Prediction (CP) struggles to balance temporal adaptability and structural stability. Feedback-driven methods (e.g., Adaptive Conformal Inference (ACI)) suffer from systemic marginal under-coverage and high interval variance during abrupt shifts, while temporally discounted Bayesian CP suffers from severe structural lag and uncalibrated interval bloat. We propose State-Adaptive Bayesian Conformal Prediction (SA-BCP) to achieve optimal spatio-temporal decoupling. By gating long-term temporal inertia with spatial kernel-density evidence, SA-BCP proactively expands intervals for recognized historical regimes while maintaining tight efficiency during stable states. We rigorously prove this mechanism's optimality, identifying a minimax bias-variance tradeoff governed by an evidence threshold $K$. Specifically, SA-BCP resolves the systematic under-coverage inherent to ACI variants while simultaneously reducing the uncalibrated interval bloat of Bayesian CP by 10\% to 37\% under high-confidence requests. ### [90] [Fairness of Classifiers in the Presence of Constraints between Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00592)
*Martin C. Cooper,Imane Bousdira*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出机器学习公平性的新定义：决策应具有"公平解释"，即不含受保护特征的素蕴涵原因。研究发现忽略特征间约束会彻底改变公平性判断，即使受保护与不受保护特征间无直接约束。论文形式化定义了分类器公平性的三种标准，分析了它们之间的关系及检验的计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统公平性定义要求决策不依赖性别等受保护特征，但当特征间存在约束时，这种依赖性可能被掩盖，导致看似公平实则歧视的决策。现有方法忽略了约束对公平性的影响，亟需建立考虑约束条件的更严谨公平性定义。

Method: 提出"公平解释"概念：决策的素蕴涵原因中不包含任何受保护特征（约束条件被纳入素蕴涵定义）。在此基础上，形式化定义了分类器公平性的三种标准：(1)所有决策仅存在公平解释；(2)所有决策至少存在一个公平解释；(3)改变受保护特征不改变决策结果。通过理论分析揭示这三个定义之间的关系，并计算检验各类公平性的计算复杂度。

Result: 识别出三种公平性定义之间的逻辑关系，并系统研究了检验这些公平性的计算复杂度。关键发现是：忽略特征间约束会完全颠覆公平性判断，即使在受保护与不受保护特征间不存在直接约束的情况下也是如此。

Conclusion: 约束条件在公平性定义中至关重要，忽视约束会导致严重的公平性误判。提出的基于公平解释的框架为机器学习公平性提供了更严谨的理论基础，三种定义对应不同程度的公平性要求，其计算复杂度分析为实际应用提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In Machine Learning, an accepted definition of fairness of a decision taken by a classifier is that it should not depend on protected features, such as gender. Unfortunately, when constraints exist between features, such dependencies can be obscured by the constraints.
  To avoid this problem, we propose that a decision be considered fair if it has a fair explanation. We define a fair explanation as a prime-implicant reason for the decision that does not contain any protected feature (where the constraints are taken into account in the definition of prime-implicant). Surprisingly, ignoring constraints can completely change the fairness of a decision (according to this definition) even in the absence of constraints between protected and unprotected features.
  Three possible definitions of fairness of a classifier are that for all its decisions (1) there are only fair explanations, (2) there is at least one fair explanation, or (3) changing protected features does not change the outcome. We identify the relationships between these different definitions of fairness and study the computational complexity of testing fairness of classifiers.

</details>

Multimodal VAEs have made progress in capturing such inter-modal dependencies by introducing a shared latent generator and a joint inference model. However, both the shared latent generator and joint inference model are parameterized as unimodal Gaussian (or Laplace), which severely limits their ability to approximate the complex structure induced by multimodal data. In this work, we study the learning problem of the multimodal EBM, shared latent generator, and joint inference model. ### [94] [RunAgent: Interpreting Natural-Language Plans with Constraint-Guided Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00798)

Abstract: Humans solve problems by executing targeted plans, yet large language models (LLMs) remain unreliable for structured workflow execution. We propose RunAgent, a multi-agent plan execution platform that interprets natural-language plans while enforcing stepwise execution through constraints and rubrics. RunAgent bridges the expressiveness of natural language with the determinism of programming via an agentic language with explicit control constructs (e.g., \texttt{IF}, \texttt{GOTO}, \texttt{FORALL}). Beyond verifying syntactic and semantic verification of the step output, which is performed based on the specific instruction of each step, RunAgent autonomously derives and validates constraints based on the description of the task and its instance at each step. RunAgent also dynamically selects among LLM-based reasoning, tool usage, and code generation and execution (e.g., in Python), and incorporates error correction mechanisms to ensure correctness. Finally, RunAgent filters the context history by retaining only relevant information during the execution of each step. Evaluations on Natural-plan and SciBench Datasets demonstrate that RunAgent outperforms baseline LLMs and state-of-the-art PlanGEN methods.

Method: 提出FedHAW方法，使用超梯度（目标函数对聚合权重的梯度）在线更新聚合权重，该计算具有较低的计算开销。

Result: 仿真结果表明，所提方法在异构环境中具有高泛化性能，并对通信错误表现出高鲁棒性。

Conclusion: FedHAW通过超梯度动态调整聚合权重，有效解决了联邦学习在异构数据分布和变化通信环境下的适应性问题，是一种计算高效且性能优越的联邦学习框架。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出AdaMeZO，一种零阶优化器，在不存储动量的情况下利用Adam风格的一阶和二阶动量估计来指导参数更新，从而适应不同曲率的损失landscape。

Abstract: Fine-tuning LLMs is necessary for various dedicated downstream tasks, but classic backpropagation-based fine-tuning methods require substantial GPU memory. Standard solutions, such as Adam, explore loss landscapes by estimating the first- and second-order moments and storing them in memory to guide the model's movement through dimensions with lower curvature and vice versa. However, directly applying Adam negates MeZO's advantage as it will triple the memory requirement. In light of this, we propose AdaMeZO, a zeroth-order optimizer that leverages Adam-style first- and second-moment estimates without maintaining them in memory. We present a theoretical analysis of AdaMeZO, corroborated by extensive experiments demonstrating AdaMeZO's performance, showing that AdaMeZO can outperform MeZO while requiring up to $70\%$ fewer forward passes. Trajectory visualizations affirm AdaMeZO's ability to adapt to diverse loss landscapes.

### [99] [Meritocratic Fairness in Budgeted Combinatorial Multi-armed Bandits via Shapley Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00762)
*Shradha Sharma,Swapnil Dhamal,Shweta Jain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对预算组合多臂老虎机完全反馈问题提出了一种公平性框架。核心创新是将合作博弈论中的夏普利值扩展为K-夏普利值，以在仅观测到总奖励的场景下度量单个臂的贡献。K-SVFair-FBF算法自适应地估计未知估值函数的K-夏普利值，在完全反馈设定下学习并抑制蒙特卡洛近似噪声，理论证明其公平性遗憾界为O(T^(3/4))，在联邦学习和社交影响力最大化数据集上验证了其公平性和有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统半反馈机制可获得单个臂的贡献，而完全反馈仅提供所选臂的总奖励，这一设定更具挑战性且更贴近实际应用。现有文献缺乏在预算约束组合老虎机中实现精英公平性的方法，标准算法无法处理完全反馈下的公平性学习问题。

Method: 1) 将经典夏普利值扩展为K-夏普利值，刻画臂在大小不超过K的子集中的边际贡献，并证明其满足对称性、线性性、零玩家性和效率性四个公理的唯一解概念；2) 提出K-SVFair-FBF公平感知算法，通过自适应估计未知估值函数的K-夏普利值，在完全反馈下学习估值函数并缓解蒙特卡洛近似带来的噪声。

Result: 理论层面：证明K-SVFair-FBF算法在公平性遗憾上达到O(T^(3/4))的遗憾界；实验层面：在联邦学习和社交影响力最大化数据集上，该算法不仅实现了公平性，而且性能优于现有基线方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的K-夏普利值框架与K-SVFair-FBF算法有效解决了完全反馈预算组合老虎机中的公平性问题，为联邦学习、社交影响力等实际应用提供了兼顾公平与效率的理论保证和实践方案。

Abstract: We propose a new framework for meritocratic fairness in budgeted combinatorial multi-armed bandits with full-bandit feedback (BCMAB-FBF). Unlike semi-bandit feedback, the contribution of individual arms is not received in full-bandit feedback, making the setting significantly more challenging. To compute arm contributions in BCMAB-FBF, we first extend the Shapley value, a classical solution concept from cooperative game theory, to the $K$-Shapley value, which captures the marginal contribution of an agent restricted to a set of size at most $K$. We show that $K$-Shapley value is a unique solution concept that satisfies Symmetry, Linearity, Null player, and efficiency properties. We next propose K-SVFair-FBF, a fairness-aware bandit algorithm that adaptively estimates $K$-Shapley value with unknown valuation function. Unlike standard bandit literature on full bandit feedback, K-SVFair-FBF not only learns the valuation function under full feedback setting but also mitigates the noise arising from Monte Carlo approximations. Theoretically, we prove that K-SVFair-FBF achieves $O(T^{3/4})$ regret bound on fairness regret. Through experiments on federated learning and social influence maximization datasets, we demonstrate that our approach achieves fairness and performs more effectively than existing baselines.

### [102] [Scaling Federated Linear Contextual Bandits via Sketching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00500)
*Hantao Yang,Hong Xie,Xutong Liu,Defu Lian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对联邦上下文线性老虎机中高维数据导致的O(d³)计算和O(d²)通信瓶颈，本文提出FSCLB，通过SVD和双草图策略将复杂度降至O(l²d)和O(ld)，实验显示成本降低90%以上且奖励损失可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在联邦上下文线性老虎机中，高数据维度引发 prohibitive 的计算与通信开销：本地智能体需执行O(d³)时间的行列式计算并上传O(d²)参数，使得现有算法难以扩展。

Method: 提出Federated Sketch Contextual Linear Bandits (FSCLB)：计算层面使用SVD间接求解行列式，将复杂度从O(d³)降至O(l²d)；通信层面采用双草图策略，将上传下载成本从O(d²)降至O(ld)；关键技术上，通过以草图矩阵替代协方差矩阵进行通信决策，解决草图更新破坏局部增量与异步通信条件的问题。

Result: 理论获得Õ((√d+√(Mε_l))√lT)的遗憾界，其中ε_l由协方差矩阵谱尾界定；当l超过矩阵秩时，界简化为Õ(√ldT)，与无草图最优遗憾界一致。合成与真实数据集实验表明，FSCLB在计算和通信成本上降低90%以上，仅牺牲可忽略的累积奖励。

Conclusion: FSCLB有效缓解了联邦上下文线性老虎机中的维度灾难问题，在计算和通信效率上实现数量级提升，同时保持理论最优性，为高维联邦学习提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: In federated contextual linear bandits, high data dimensionality incurs prohibitive computation and communication costs: local agents perform $O(d^3)$-time determinant computation and upload $O(d^2)$ parameters, making existing algorithms unscalable, where $d$ is the dimension of data. To relieve these scaling bottlenecks, this paper proposes Federated Sketch Contextual Linear Bandits (FSCLB). On the computation side, FSCLB uses SVD to indirectly obtain the determinant required for communication, eliminating the prohibitive cost of direct determinant calculation and cutting complexity from $O(d^3)$ to $O(l^2d)$ per round, where $l< d$ is the sketch size. On the communication side, FSCLB introduces a double-sketch strategy that reduces both upload and download costs from $O(d^2)$ to $O(ld)$. Naively involving sketch update into federated contextual linear bandits can destroy the local increment and invalidate the asynchronous communication condition; FSCLB solves this by replacing the covariance matrix with the sketch matrix when deciding whether to communicate. Theoretically, FSCLB achieves a regret bound of $\widetilde{O} ((\sqrt{d}+\sqrt{M\varepsilon_l})\sqrt{lT})$, where $\varepsilon_l$ is the upper bounded by the spectral tail of the covariance matrix; when $l$ exceeds the rank of the covariance matrix, the bound simplifies to $\widetilde{O}(\sqrt{ldT})$, matching the optimal no-sketch regret. Experiments on both synthetic and real-world datasets show that FSCLB significantly reduces computational and communication costs by over 90 \% while sacrificing only a negligible amount of cumulative reward.

</details>


### [103] [LambdaRankIC: Directly Optimizing Rank IC for Financial Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00501)
*Yan Lin,Yihong Su,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对金融预测中训练目标与Rank IC评估指标不对齐的问题，本文提出LambdaRankIC，通过推导成对排序交换的lambda梯度闭式解直接优化Rank IC，在XGBoost中实现并验证其理论可优化Rank IC上界，在模拟和实证数据上均优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出LambdaRankIC学习排序框架，通过解析推导成对样本排序交换产生的lambda梯度闭式表达式，解决排序算子不可微问题。将LambdaRankIC实现为XGBoost的自定义目标函数，利用梯度下降高效优化。理论证明该目标函数可优化Rank IC的上界。

Result: 模拟实验表明，LambdaRankIC在无噪声环境下能准确恢复真实排序，在低信噪比和重尾噪声条件下显著优于回归和NDCG方法。真实市场数据验证显示，LambdaRankIC在Rank IC、ICIR、月度收益率和夏普比率等关键金融指标上均取得最优样本外表现。

Conclusion: 直接优化Rank IC可显著提升金融预测性能，LambdaRankIC有效弥合了训练目标与评估指标的鸿沟，为以完整排序质量为核心目标的金融预测任务提供了更优解决方案。

Abstract: In financial predictions, the performance of machine learning models is often assessed by Rank IC, which is the Spearman rank correlation between the model predictions and the realized asset returns. Despite its wide adoption, most existing models are trained using regression losses or ranking objectives that may not align with Rank IC. We propose LambdaRankIC, a novel learning-to-rank approach that directly optimizes Rank IC. We circumvent the non-differentiability of the ranking operator by deriving the closed-form expression for the lambda gradients induced by the pairwise rank swaps, which enables efficient gradient-based optimization within the LambdaRank framework. We implement LambdaRankIC as a custom objective in XGBoost. Theoretically, we show that our approach optimizes an upper bound on Rank IC. We evaluate the proposed approach on both simulated and real-world financial data. In simulation studies, LambdaRankIC accurately recovers the true ranking structure in noiseless settings and consistently outperforms regression-based and NDCG-oriented ranking methods under low signal-to-noise ratios and heavy-tailed noise regimes. In empirical experiments using real market data, LambdaRankIC achieves the best out-of-sample performance on evaluation metrics commonly used in finance, including Rank IC, ICIR, monthly return, and Sharpe ratio. These results show that directly optimizing Rank IC can yield substantial improvements over conventional learning objectives in financial predictions when the full-order ranking quality is the primary goal.

*Andrs Formanek,Anna Vincze,Richrd Bicsak,Yves Moreau,Gyorgy T. Balogh,Adam Arany*

TL;DR: 本研究构建了一个包含143个药物分子的多任务数据集，涵盖6种不同模型膜的PAMPA渗透性数据，系统评估了从线性回归到预训练Transformer等多种预测模型，揭示了在有限样本条件下专家设计的理化描述符优于深度学习表示。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在系统评估不同分子描述符和机器学习模型在预测被动膜渗透性中的效能，探究预测精度与模型可解释性之间的权衡关系，并识别机器学习方法在该领域面临的特殊挑战，同时建立首个多器官特异性PAMPA膜的综合性研究框架。

Method: 研究创建了一个独特的143个药物/候选分子组成的多任务数据集，通过体外平行人工膜渗透性测定(PAMPA)在6种不同模型膜上进行实验评估。采用系统性比较策略，涵盖从简单线性回归到现代预训练Transformer架构的多种模型，重点分析性能与可解释性的平衡。

Result: 实验结果表明，在样本量有限的情况下，专家设计的物理化学性质描述符比基于深度学习的表示方法更适合渗透性预测。该研究是目前为止对多器官特异性PAMPA膜同时进行建模的最全面研究，为膜特异性渗透性特征提供了新的科学见解。

Conclusion: 小样本膜渗透性研究更适合采用传统专家设计的描述符而非深度学习方法。本研究不仅建立了高质量的PAMPA数据集，还揭示了不同模型膜的特异性渗透规律，为未来药物渗透性预测方法的选择提供了重要参考依据。

Abstract: We present a unique, multitask dataset comprising 143 drug and drug candidate molecules, each evaluated on in vitro, parallel artificial-membrane permeability assays (PAMPA) using six different model membranes. Using this resource, we systematically assess the effectiveness of various molecular descriptors and regression models in predicting passive membrane permeability. The studied models range from simple linear regression to a modern pre-trained transformer architecture. Particular attention is given to the trade-off between predictive performance and model interpretability, highlighting the challenges introduced by machine learning approaches. To our knowledge, this is the most comprehensive study on simultaneous modeling of multiple organ-specific PAMPA membranes to date, offering novel insights into membrane-specific permeability profiles.
  We found that expert-designed physico-chemical property descriptors are more fitting for a limited sample size permeabilty study than deep learning based representations.

### [105] [Stable-GFlowNet: Toward Diverse and Robust LLM Red-Teaming via Contrastive Trajectory Balance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00553)
*Minchan Kwon,Sunghyun Baek,Minseo Kim,Jaemyung Yu,Dongyoon Han,Junmo Kim*

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM红队测试中存在的训练不稳定和模式崩溃问题，提出Stable-GFN (S-GFN)方法。通过消除分区函数Z估计、采用成对比较、鲁棒掩码和流畅性稳定器，S-GFN在保持攻击效果的同时显著提升了训练稳定性与攻击多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Stable-GFN (S-GFN)：1) 通过成对比较消除对分区函数Z的估计，降低计算不稳定性；2) 设计鲁棒掩码机制过滤噪声奖励信号；3) 引入流畅性稳定器，避免模型陷入生成乱码的局部最优，从而在保持GFN最优策略的同时提升训练稳定性。

Result: S-GFN在多项设置下均展现出显著优势：训练过程更稳定，有效缓解了模式崩溃现象，同时实现了更优的攻击性能和攻击多样性。

Conclusion: S-GFN成功解决了GFNs在LLM红队测试中的核心缺陷，为构建安全可靠的LLM提供了更有效的红队测试工具，兼具理论创新与实践价值。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) Red-Teaming, which proactively identifies vulnerabilities of LLMs, is an essential process for ensuring safety. Finding effective and diverse attacks in red-teaming is important, but achieving both is challenging. Generative Flow Networks (GFNs) that perform distribution matching are a promising methods, but they are notorious for training instability and mode collapse. In particular, unstable rewards in red-teaming accelerate mode collapse. We propose Stable-GFN (S-GFN), which eliminates partition function $Z$ estimation in GFN and reduces training instability. S-GFN avoids Z-estimation through pairwise comparisons and employs a robust masking methodology against noisy rewards. Additionally, we propose a fluency stabilizer to prevent the model from getting stuck in local optima that produce gibberish. S-GFN provides more stable training while maintaining the optimal policy of GFN. We demonstrate the overwhelming attack performance and diversity of S-GFN across various settings.

### [106] [Decouple before Integration: Test-time Synthesis of SFT and RLVR Task Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00610)
*Chaohao Yuan,Chenghao Xiao,Yu Rong,Hong Cheng,Long-Kai Huang*

TL;DR: 本文提出DoTS，一种在测试时通过任务向量算术融合SFT和RLVR的方法，解决了两者整合中的灾难性遗忘和梯度冲突问题，仅用3%的计算成本达到或超过训练时整合方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SFT和RLVR分别擅长知识广度与推理深度，但整合时存在灾难性遗忘（顺序训练）和梯度冲突（联合优化）问题。通过任务向量分析发现两者存在30倍幅度差异、45倍符号干扰和异质化模块更新分布，难以直接整合，但修改的是模型部分互补的组件。

Method: 提出Decoupled Test-time Synthesis (DoTS)，独立训练SFT和RLVR模型，在推理时通过任务向量算术融合两者能力。采用选择性稀疏化配合保范数重缩放减少干扰，并使用贝叶斯优化在少量无标签查询上搜索一致性/困惑度的帕累托前沿组合系数。

Result: DoTS在多个数学推理基准上匹配或超越训练时整合方法，计算成本仅约3%。当应用于更强的模型检查点时，DoTS超越SOTA模型并泛化到分布外基准，无需重新调优。

Conclusion: DoTS成功实现了SFT和RLVR的解耦融合，通过测试时向量合成避免了训练冲突，以极低成本获得高性能，展示了任务向量方法在模型集成中的潜力。

Abstract: SFT and RLVR represent two fundamental yet distinct paradigms for LLM post-training, each excelling in distinct dimensions. SFT expands knowledge breadth while RLVR enhances reasoning depth. Yet integrating these complementary strengths remains a formidable challenge. Sequential training can cause catastrophic forgetting, and joint optimization often suffers from severe gradient conflicts. We analyze SFT and RLVR through the lens of task vectors and reveal three structural properties behind these failures: a 30* magnitude disparity, 45* sign interference, and heterogeneous module-wise update distributions. These findings show SFT and RLVR are difficult to integrate directly, but they also suggest that the two paradigms modify partly complementary components of the model. Motivated by these observations, we propose Decoupled Test-time Synthesis (DoTS), a post-hoc framework allows SFT and RLVR checkpoints to be trained independently and synthesizes their capabilities only at inference time via task vector arithmetic, without updating model parameters. To reduce interference, DOTS applies selective sparsification with norm-preserving rescaling. It then uses Bayesian optimization on a small set of unlabeled queries to search for combination coefficients on the Pareto frontier of consistency and perplexity. Empirically, \ours matches or exceeds the performance of training-based SFT--RLVR integration methods across multiple mathematical reasoning benchmarks, incurring only $\sim$3\% of the computational cost. When applied to stronger post-trained checkpoints, DOTS surpasses SOTA models and generalizes to out-of-domain benchmarks without re-tuning. Code is available at https://github.com/chaohaoyuan/DoTS.

### [107] [Class Angular Distortion Index for Dimensionality Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00637)
*Kaviru Gunaratne,Stephen Kobourov,Jacob Miller*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 这篇论文提出了类角度失真指数(CADI)，一种评估降维技术中类簇结构保真度的新指标。与现有指标不同，CADI通过计算点三元组之间的内部角度来衡量投影后类簇的相对位置关系，具有可微性，可用于优化降维算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有降维技术（如t-SNE和UMAP）在可视化时存在类簇相对位置任意或误导的问题，而现有的类簇质量评估指标要么仅衡量类簇可分性，要么假设原始空间中的类簇是球形的。这导致无法准确评估降维后类簇组织的保真度，需要一种更有效的评估指标。

Method: 提出Class Angular Distortion Index (CADI)，通过计算点三元组之间的内部角度来量化降维投影中类簇组织的保真度。该方法利用角度信息来评估类簇的相对排列是否被正确保留。

Result: 在真实和合成数据集上的实验表明，当现有类簇指标失效时，CADI仍能提供可解释的结果。此外，由于CADI是可微的，研究者开发了一种基于CADI的降维技术。

Conclusion: CADI是一个有效的类簇保真度评估指标，能够解决现有方法的局限性，并且由于其可微性，可以直接用于优化降维算法，为评估和改进降维技术提供了新工具。

Abstract: Dimensionality reduction (DR) techniques are often characterized by whether they preserve global, high-level structures in the data or local, neighborhood structures. This distinction matters in visualization: global methods can obscure clusters while local methods can over-emphasize them. Yet, even when clusters appear distinct, their relative arrangement in the projection may be arbitrary or misleading, a common issue in techniques such as t-SNE and UMAP. Existing cluster quality metrics either only measure cluster separability or assume spherical, globular clusters in the original space. We introduce the Class Angular Distortion Index (CADI), a metric that uses internal angles among point triples to determine the faithfulness of cluster organization in a projection. We show cases on both real and synthetic data where existing cluster metrics fail, but CADI provides an interpretable result. Since it relies on computing angles, CADI is also differentiable, enabling optimization. We demonstrate this with a CADI-based DR technique.

Prior work has mainly studied unsupervised / supervised machine unlearning, leaving unlearning for sequential decision-making systems far less understood. We initiate the first study of a foundational sequential decision-making problem: offline stochastic multi-armed bandits (MAB). We formalize the privacy constraint for offline MAB and measure utility by the post-unlearning decision quality. We conduct a systematic study of both single- and multi-source unlearning scenarios under two data-generation models, the fixed-sample model and the distribution model. For these settings, our algorithmic design is built on two canonical base algorithms: Gaussian mechanism and rollback, and we propose adaptive algorithms that switch between them according to the data regime and privacy constraint. We further introduce a mixing procedure that elucidates the rationale behind these baselines. We provide performance guarantees across the above settings and establish lower bounds under both dataset models. Experiments validate the predicted tradeoffs and demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methods.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 标准预测评估无法反映模型在临床任务中的真实效用，任务感知评估框架能揭示关键缺陷。作者开源了基准测试、标准化预处理流程及可重复的干预数据集工具包，推动临床预测模型向真正实用化方向发展。

In safety-critical settings, low average error can coexist with dangerous failures in exactly the high-risk regimes that matter most. We present a task-aware evaluation framework for blood glucose forecasting built around two downstream uses: hypoglycemia early warning and insulin dosing decision support. For early warning, we evaluate on real data from three clinical cohorts using event-level recall and false alarms per patient-day, metrics that reflect operational alarm burden rather than aggregate accuracy. We show that models appearing acceptable overall, with recall above 0.9 on the full test set, can fail badly in the post-bolus slice, where insulin-on-board is elevated and missed warnings carry the greatest clinical consequences. Standard forecasting evaluation, however, does not test whether a model can reason about the effects of actions, a requirement for supporting insulin dosing decisions. We therefore add a second, interventional arm using the FDA-accepted UVA/Padova simulator, where we evaluate whether forecasters can predict glucose responses to altered insulin plans in paired factual/counterfactual scenarios. We show that models that look strong on real-data forecasting often fail to predict the direction, magnitude, or ranking of intervention effects, and choose poor insulin doses when evaluated under a clinically motivated cost. Taken together, the two arms reveal a consistent gap between forecasting accuracy and task-relevant usefulness. We release the benchmark, the standardized preprocessing pipeline for public cohorts, and the simulator-based interventional dataset as a reproducible toolkit.

### [110] [PEACE: Cross-modal Enhanced Pediatric-Adult ECG Alignment for Robust Pediatric Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00647)
*Xinran Liu,Yuwen Li,Hongxiang Gao,Heyang Xu,Jianqing Li,Zongmin Wang,Chengyu Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对儿童心电图诊断中标注数据稀缺和成人模型跨群体泛化能力差的问题，本文提出PEACE框架，通过跨模态对齐实现成人到儿童的心电迁移学习，利用大型语言模型生成标签条件化的语义描述作为辅助监督，在零样本、少样本和微调设置下分别达到59.39%、79.03%和90.89%的AUC，为低资源儿童心电诊断提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出PEACE（Pediatric-Adult ECG Alignment via Cross-modal Enhancement）框架，包含三个核心组件：1）三轴临床语义分解，将心电图特征分解为多个语义维度；2）标签查询特征提取，利用标签信息引导特征对齐；3）课程门控优化，逐步优化迁移过程。针对ZZU-pECG数据集缺乏配对临床报告的问题，采用Gemini模型生成标签条件化的语义描述作为辅助监督信号，但在推理时仅使用心电图信号，保持临床实用性。

Result: 在ZZU-pECG数据集上，PEACE框架在零样本、50样本和全微调设置下分别达到59.39%、79.03%和90.89%的AUC值；在共享的PTB-XL标签空间上达到96.65%的AUC。这些结果表明结构化临床语义监督能显著改善低资源成人到儿童的ECG迁移效果。

Conclusion: 结构化临床语义监督是提升低资源成人到儿童心电图迁移学习的有效策略。但研究仍存在局限，未来需要开展前瞻性临床验证，并设计更明确的年龄感知建模方法，才能推动该方法在真实临床场景中的部署应用。

Abstract: Automated pediatric electrocardiogram (ECG) diagnosis remains challenging because models trained predominantly on adult data suffer from substantial cross-population mismatch, while pediatric labels are often scarce. We present PEACE (Pediatric-Adult ECG Alignment via Cross-modal Enhancement), a structured cross-modal alignment framework for adult-to-pediatric ECG transfer. PEACE integrates tri-axial clinical semantic decomposition, label-query feature extraction, and curriculum-gated optimization to align transferable adult ECG representations with pediatric diagnostic targets. Since ZZU-pECG provides no paired clinical reports, we generate label-conditioned semantic descriptors using Gemini with concise clinical prompts and use them only as auxiliary training supervision; inference remains ECG-only. On ZZU-pECG, PEACE achieves 59.39%, 79.03%, and 90.89% AUC under zero-shot, 50-shot, and full fine-tuning settings, respectively, and reaches 96.65% AUC on the shared PTB-XL label space. These results suggest that structured clinical semantic supervision can improve low-resource adult-to-pediatric ECG transfer, while prospective clinical validation and more explicit age-aware modeling remain necessary before real-world deployment.

### [111] [Budget Constraints as Riemannian Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00649)
*Michael Helcig,Dan Alistarh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出黎曼约束优化(RCO)，通过在logit空间的黎曼流形上进行切线投影、二分搜索收缩和动量传输，实现预算约束下真实目标函数的一阶优化，在合成背包问题和LLM压缩任务上显著优于惩罚方法和进化搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习中的混合精度量化、非均匀剪枝和专家选择等问题可归结为在总成本预算下为N个组分配K个选项的组合优化问题。由于目标函数（模型损失）不能分解到各组，组合求解器无法直接优化真实目标，而进化搜索缺乏梯度信息，惩罚方法只能近似满足预算且需要敏感的超参数调优。

Method: 基于softmax松弛下预算约束在logit空间形成具有简单几何结构的光滑黎曼流形这一发现，提出RCO方法：将标准Adam更新通过切线投影、沿成本向量二分搜索收缩（精确满足预算）和单次内积动量传输进行增强，并结合Gumbel straight-through估计和预算约束动态规划处理离散可行性。

Result: 在合成背包问题上，RCO能恢复最优解，而惩罚方法仅能达到83%的最优性能。在LLM压缩任务中，RCO匹配或超越进化搜索方法，同时墙钟时间降低3-16倍。

Conclusion: RCO利用黎曼流形的几何特性，实现了预算约束下真实目标函数的高效一阶优化，具有精确预算执行、无需约束超参数和计算效率高等优势，为资源受限的模型压缩提供了新范式。

Abstract: Assigning one of K options to each of N groups under a total cost budget is a recurring problem in machine learning, appearing in mixed-precision quantization, non-uniform pruning, and expert selection. The objective (model loss) depends jointly on all assignments and does not decompose across groups, which prevents combinatorial solvers from optimizing the true objective directly and limits them to proxy objectives. Evolutionary search evaluates the actual loss but lacks gradient information, while penalty-based methods provide gradients but enforce the budget only approximately and require sensitive hyperparameter tuning. We observe that under softmax relaxation, the budget constraint defines a smooth Riemannian manifold in logit space with particularly simple geometry: the normal vector is available in closed form, shifting logits along the cost vector changes expected cost monotonically, allowing binary-search retraction, and vector transport reduces to a single inner product. Building on this structure, we propose Riemannian Constrained Optimization (RCO), which augments a standard Adam update with tangent projection, binary-search retraction, and momentum transport. Combined with Gumbel straight-through estimation and budget-constrained dynamic programming for discrete feasibility, RCO enables first-order optimization of the true objective under exact budget enforcement, without introducing constraint hyperparameters. On synthetic knapsack problems with known optima, the manifold-based constraint handling recovers optimal solutions, whereas penalty methods plateau at 83% of optimal. On LLM compression tasks, including mixed-precision quantization and MoE expert pruning, RCO matches or exceeds evolutionary search methods while requiring 3x to 16x lower wall-clock cost on the evaluated configurations.

</details>


### [112] [Evaluating the Architectural Reasoning Capabilities of LLM Provers via the Obfuscated Natural Number Game](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00677)
*Lixing Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过混淆标识符构建零知识数学环境，提出"架构推理"新基准，揭示通用模型与专用推理模型在真实逻辑能力上的本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在形式化数学基准测试中表现优异，但无法确定其成就是源于真正的逻辑推理能力还是对预训练数据的语义模式匹配。为未来自动定理发现AI建立可评估真实推理能力的量化标准成为关键需求。

Method: 在Lean 4环境中创建"混淆自然数游戏"基准，通过重命名所有标识符构建零知识封闭域。评估Claude-Sonnet-4.5、GPT-4o、DeepSeek-R1、GPT-5、DeepSeek-Prover-V2等先进模型，对比其在原始与混淆环境下的性能差异与推理时延。

Result: 发现所有模型均存在"延迟代价"——混淆环境导致推理时间普遍增加。性能表现出现显著分化：通用模型性能下降，而专用推理模型在无cue情况下准确率保持稳定，证明其具备基于局部公理的真实推理能力。

Conclusion: 该研究为评估数学推理能力提供了量化度量标准，区分了记忆依赖型与逻辑推导型模型的本质差异，为开发具有真正定理发现能力的人工智能奠定了评估基础。

Abstract: While Large Language Models have achieved notable success on formal mathematics benchmarks such as MiniF2F, it remains unclear whether these results stem from genuine logical reasoning or semantic pattern matching against pre-training data. This paper identifies Architectural Reasoning: the ability to synthesize formal proofs using exclusively local axioms and definitions within an alien math domain, as the necessary ability for future automated theorem discovery AI. We use the Obfuscated Natural Number Game, a benchmark to evaluate Architectural Reasoning. By renaming identifiers in the Natural Number Game in Lean 4, we created a zero-knowledge, closed environment. We evaluate state-of-the-art models, finding a universal latency tax where obfuscation increases inference time. The results also reveal a divergence in robustness: while general models (Claude-Sonnet-4.5, GPT-4o) suffer performance degradation, reasoning models (DeepSeek-R1, GPT-5, DeepSeek-Prover-V2) maintain the same accuracy despite the absence of semantic cues. These findings provide a quantitative metric for assessing the true capacity for mathematical reasoning.

</details>


### [113] [Deep Kernel Learning for Stratifying Glaucoma Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00708)
*Bruce Rushing,Angela Danquah,Alireza Namazi,Arjun Dirghangi,Heman Shakeri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对青光眼等慢性病患者风险分层难题，本研究提出一种新型深度核学习框架，结合高斯过程与基于临床BERT嵌入的Transformer特征提取器，成功从稀疏不规则的电子健康记录中识别出三个临床亚组，并发现高风险组在视力较好的情况下仍呈现恶化趋势，为临床决策提供了有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在青光眼等慢性疾病管理中，如何从稀疏且不规则采样的电子健康记录中有效识别高风险进展患者是重大临床挑战。现有方法往往只能反映患者当前疾病状态，难以预测未来风险轨迹，导致无法实现早期针对性干预。

Method: 提出一种深度核学习（DKL）架构，采用高斯过程作为后端。该模型的核心创新在于使用Transformer特征提取器处理临床-BERT嵌入，构建高斯过程的核函数，从而对多模态电子健康记录中的患者病程轨迹进行建模。

Result: 该方法成功识别出三个临床特征显著不同的患者亚组。关键发现是模型能够解耦疾病进展与当前严重程度，识别出一组尽管平均视力优于另一组稳定差视力患者，但仍呈现恶化轨迹的高风险群体，证明模型学习的是进展风险而非仅仅是当前疾病状态。

Conclusion: 本研究开发的风险分层模型能够有效预测慢性病患者未来进展轨迹，为临床决策支持提供了有力工具。通过识别高风险患者实现靶向干预，可改善青光眼等慢性病的治疗管理，具有重要的临床转化价值。

Abstract: Effectively stratifying patient risk in chronic diseases like glaucoma is a major clinical challenge. Clinicians need tools to identify patients at high risk of progression from sparse and irregularly-sampled electronic health records (EHRs). We propose a novel deep kernel learning (DKL) architecture that leverages a Gaussian Process (GP) backend. The GP's kernel is defined by a transformer-based feature extractor applied to clinical-BERT embeddings to model glaucoma patient trajectories from multimodal EHR data. Our method successfully identifies three clinically distinct patient subgroups. Crucially, the model learns to decouple disease progression from current severity, identifying a high-risk group with a worsening trajectory despite having better average visual acuity than a second, stably poor group. This reveals that the model learns to identify progression risk rather than just the current disease state. This ability to stratify patients based on their risk trajectory progression offers a powerful tool for clinical decision support, enabling targeted interventions for high-risk individuals and improving the management of glaucoma care.

### [114] [Temporal Data Requirement for Predicting Unplanned Hospital Readmissions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00738)
*Ramin Mohammadi,Vahab vahdat,Sarthak Jain,Amir T. Namin,Ramya Palacholla,Sagar Kamarthi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了电子健康记录中历史数据时间窗口对预测髋膝关节置换术后30天再入院的影响，发现临床笔记的最佳观察窗口仅为术前3-6个月，而有结构数据窗口可达12个月，挑战了"数据越多越好"的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着电子健康记录(EHR)的普及，构建预测模型时面临的关键挑战是确定最大化准确性的最佳历史数据时间窗口，现有研究缺乏针对医疗数据模态特性的时间窗口优化指南。

Method: 研究纳入7,174例患者的400余万条结构化疗程记录和8万条非结构化临床笔记，测试从手术当天至术前3年的多种观察窗口；采用BOW、TF-IDF、LDA等非神经编码器和BERT、1D CNN、BiLSTM等神经编码器提取文本特征，分别评估纯笔记、纯结构化数据及多模态融合模型的预测性能。

Result: 非结构化临床笔记的最佳预测性能仅出现在术前3-6个月的时间窗口，而有结构数据性能随窗口延长而提升，但在12个月后严格趋于平稳；该模态特异性时间模式在不同模型复杂度和编码器类型下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 研究发现历史数据量并非越多越好，不同数据模态存在最优时间窗口阈值；为再入院预测模型提供了针对性的时间窗口优化指南，对EHR预测建模具有普适性参考价值。

Abstract: With the proliferation of Electronic Health Records (EHRs), a critical challenge in building predictive models is determining the optimal historical data time window to maximize accuracy. This study investigates the impact of various observation windows ranging from the day of surgery to three years prior on predicting 30-day readmission following hip and knee arthroplasties. The dataset encompasses both structured encounter records (over 4 million) and unstructured clinical notes (80,000) from 7,174 patients. To extract meaning from the clinical notes, we employed a suite of non neural (BOW, count BOW, TF IDF, LDA) and neural encoders (BERT, 1D CNN, BiLSTM, Average). We subsequently evaluated models utilizing clinical notes alone, structured data alone, and a combination of both modalities. Our results demonstrate that the optimal time window for unstructured clinical notes is significantly shorter than for structured data, maximum predictive performance was achieved using notes from just three to six months prior to surgery. In contrast, performance using structured data improved as the time window lengthened, but strictly plateaued after twelve months. These modality-specific temporal patterns remained consistent regardless of model complexity or encoder type. Ultimately, these findings challenge the general assumption that more historical data inherently yields better machine learning predictions, establishing targeted time-window guidelines for optimizing readmission prediction models.

### [115] [SAVGO: Learning State-Action Value Geometry with Cosine Similarity for Continuous Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00787)
*Stavros Orfanoudakis,Pedro P. Vergara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 一篇论文提出了一种名为SAVGO的几何感知强化学习算法，该算法通过将基于价值函数的动作相似性直接引入策略更新来解决现有表示学习方法在动作空间应用不足的问题。该算法学习一个联合状态-动作嵌入空间，使得具有相似动作价值估计的样本对具有高余弦相似度，而不同样本对则被映射到不同方向。这种学习到的几何结构支持在每次更新时生成候选动作的相似性核，从而指导策略改进直接朝向更高价值区域，超越了传统的局部梯度更新。方法将表示学习、价值估计和策略优化统一在一个几何一致的目标中，同时在离线策略演员-评论家训练框架下保持可扩展性。在MuJoCo连续控制基准测试中，该方法在挑战性的高维任务上表现优于强基线算法，消融实验验证了价值几何学习和基于相似性的策略更新的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管表示学习和相似性学习提高了强化学习的样本效率，但它们很少被用于直接在动作空间中塑造策略更新。为解决这一空白，论文提出了一种几何感知的强化学习算法SAVGO，旨在将基于价值函数的相似性显式地融入策略更新过程。

Method: 论文提出SAVGO算法，其核心方法包括：1) 学习一个联合状态-动作嵌入空间，在该空间中，具有相似动作价值估计的样本对表现出高余弦相似度，而相异样本对被映射到不同方向；2) 基于学习到的几何结构，在每次策略更新时为采样的候选动作生成相似性核；3) 利用该相似性核指导策略改进直接朝向更高价值区域，超越局部梯度更新；4) 将表示学习、价值估计和策略优化统一在单个几何一致的目标函数中，同时保持离线策略演员-评论家训练的可扩展性。

Result: 在标准MuJoCo连续控制基准测试上的评估表明，SAVGO在具有挑战性的高维任务上相比强基线算法表现出显著改进。消融实验进一步分析了价值几何学习和基于相似性的策略更新各自的贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将表示学习、价值估计和策略优化统一在一个几何一致的框架中，证明了将价值函数几何结构显式引入策略更新的有效性。SAVGO算法不仅提高了高维连续控制任务的性能，还保持了离线策略训练的可扩展性，为未来强化学习算法设计提供了新的几何感知思路。

Abstract: While representation and similarity learning have improved the sample efficiency of Reinforcement Learning (RL), they are rarely used to shape policy updates directly in the action space. To bridge this gap, a geometry-aware RL algorithm that explicitly incorporates value-based similarity into the policy update, State-Action Value Geometry Optimization (SAVGO), is proposed. In detail, SAVGO learns a joint state-action embedding space in which pairs with similar action-value estimates exhibit high cosine similarity, while dissimilar pairs are mapped to distinct directions. This learned geometry enables the generation of a similarity kernel over candidate actions sampled at each update, allowing policy improvement to be guided directly toward higher-value regions beyond local gradient-based updates. As a result, representation learning, value estimation, and policy optimization are unified within a single geometry-consistent objective, while preserving the scalability of off-policy actor-critic training. The proposed method is evaluated on standard MuJoCo continuous-control benchmarks, demonstrating improvements over strong baselines on challenging high-dimensional tasks. Ablation studies are done to analyze the contributions of value-geometry learning and similarity-based policy updates.

</details>


### [116] [Generating Statistical Charts with Validation-Driven LLM Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00800)
*Pavlin G. Poličar,Andraž Pevcin,Blaž Zupan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出结构化LLM工作流解决表格数据生成可读图表的挑战，通过七阶段流程（数据集筛选、绘图提案、代码合成、渲染、验证优化、描述生成、问答生成）并加入渲染验证机制，生成了含1500个图表和30003个问答对的数据集，评估16个多模态模型发现图表语法问题已近饱和而数值推理仍具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM图表生成的失败模式仅在渲染后显现且无法从代码或数据本身检测，同时公开数据集缺乏可执行代码、数据集上下文与问答对等完整对齐资源，限制了对可视化失败机制的深入理解和模型诊断评估。

Method: 设计七阶段结构化工作流：1) 数据集筛选；2) 绘图提案；3) 代码合成；4) 渲染；5) 验证驱动优化（解决可读性与语义不匹配）；6) 图表描述生成；7) 问答对生成。核心创新是将图表生成视为可检查过程而非一次性提示转代码任务，每个产出物均保留完整溯源信息。

Result: 在UCI数据集上构建大规模资源：74个原始数据集生成1500个图表，涵盖24种图表家族，配套30003个问答对。对16个多模态大模型的评估表明，图表语法类问题性能接近饱和（近乎解决），而数值提取、比较和推理任务仍具显著挑战性，揭示了当前MLLM的能力边界。

Conclusion: 该工作流为图表生成提供了可检查、可复现的研究框架，所创建的数据集能有效诊断多模态模型在图表 grounded 推理中的薄弱环节，对推动可视化理解与推理的精细化评估具有重要方法论价值和实践意义。

Abstract: Generating diverse, readable statistical charts from tabular data remains challenging for LLMs, as many failures become apparent after rendering and are not detectable from data or code alone. Existing chart datasets also rarely provide fully aligned artifacts, such as executable code, dataset context, and question-answer pairs. We present a structured LLM-based workflow that decomposes chart generation into dataset screening, plot proposal, code synthesis, rendering, validation-driven refinement, description generation, and question-answer generation. By incorporating rendered-output validation, the workflow addresses visualization-specific failure modes such as readability and semantic mismatch. It treats chart generation as an inspectable process rather than a one-shot prompt-to-code task, retaining each chart with its code, dataset context, description, and question-answer pairs. Applied to UCI datasets, the workflow produces 1,500 charts from 74 datasets, spanning 24 chart families and paired with 30,003 question-answer pairs. We evaluate 16 multimodal LLMs (MLLMs) on these chart-question pairs. The results show that chart-syntax questions are nearly saturated, while value extraction, comparison, and reasoning remain more challenging, illustrating the workflow's utility for diagnostic studies of chart-grounded multimodal reasoning.

</details>

### [117] [A Survey of Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval: Progress and Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00063)
*Yiyang Wei,Tingyu Song,Siyue Zhang,Yilun Zhao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三管齐下方法：(1)按知识领域和模态系统化RIR基准测试；(2)基于推理集成位置与方式构建结构化分类法；(3)分析挑战与未来方向。

Abstract: Reasoning-Intensive Retrieval (RIR) targets retrieval settings where relevance is mediated by latent inferential links between a query and supporting evidence, rather than semantic similarity. Motivated by the emergent reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), recent work integrates these capabilities into the IR field, spanning the entire pipeline from benchmarks to retrievers and rerankers. Despite this progress, the field lacks a systematic framework to organize current efforts and articulate a clear path forward. To provide a clear roadmap for this rapidly growing yet fragmented area, this survey (1) systematizes existing RIR benchmarks by knowledge domains and modalities, providing a detailed analysis of the current landscape; (2) introduces a structured taxonomy that categorizes methods based on where and how reasoning is integrated into the retrieval pipeline, alongside an analysis of their trade-offs and practical applications; and (3) summarizes challenges and future directions to guide research in this evolving field.

### [118] [Intelligent Elastic Feature Fading: Enabling Model Retrain-Free Feature Efficiency Rollouts at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00324)
*Jieming Di,Xiaoyu Chen,Ying She,Siyu Wang,Lizzie Liu,Fenggang Wu,Jiaoying Mu,Tony Tsui,Amr Elroumy,Hsing Tang,Zewei Jiang,Qiao Yang,Lin Qi,Haibo Lin,Weifeng Cui,Daniel Li,Kapil Gupta,Shivendra Pratap Singh,Jie Zheng,Arnold Overwijk,Ling Leng,Sri Reddy,Robert Malkin,Rocky Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对大规模排序系统特征重训导致迭代周期长、GPU开销大、发布吞吐量低的问题，本文提出智能弹性特征衰减（IEFF）系统，通过服务时弹性控制特征覆盖实现免重训发布，实现5倍发布加速、GPU开销归零，并减少50-55%性能衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模排序系统依赖成千上万跨时间周期的用户行为特征，但特征变更需完整模型重训，导致3-6个月迭代周期、巨大GPU资源消耗和受限发布吞吐量，严重制约特征效率优化的敏捷性。

Method: 提出智能弹性特征衰减（IEFF）生产基础设施系统，核心是在服务时弹性调控特征覆盖率与分布，配合持续训练机制使模型自适应特征变化，消除显式重训依赖。系统集成严格安全护栏、可逆机制和全方位监控，确保大规模部署稳定性。

Result: 多生产场景显示，IEFF将效率发布加速5倍，完全消除重训GPU开销，加速容量回收。离线与在线实验证实，渐进式特征衰减相比突然移除特征可避免50-55%在线性能下降，同时维持模型行为稳定。

Conclusion: 弹性系统级特征衰减为现代工业排序系统特征效率管理提供实用可扩展方案，通过系统层面创新实现特征管理敏捷性与资源效率的显著提升，是免重训特征发布的有效实践。

Abstract: Large-scale ranking systems depend on thousands of features derived from user behavior across multiple time horizons. Typically requires model retraining -- resulting in long iteration cycles (3--6 months), substantial GPU resource consumption, and limited rollout throughput.
  We introduce Intelligent Elastic Feature Fading (IEFF), a production infrastructure system that enables retrain-free feature efficiency rollouts by elastically controlling feature coverage and distribution at serving time. IEFF supports incremental feature coverage adjustments while models adapt through recurring training, eliminating dependencies on explicit retraining cycles. The system incorporates strict safety guardrails, reversibility mechanisms, and comprehensive monitoring to ensure stability at scale.
  Across multiple production use cases, IEFF accelerates efficiency-related rollouts by 5$\times$, eliminates retraining-related GPU overhead, and enables faster capacity recycling. Extensive offline and online experiments demonstrate that gradual feature fading prevents 50--55\% of online performance degradation compared to abrupt feature removal, while maintaining stable model behavior. These results establish elastic, system-level feature fading as a practical and scalable approach for managing feature efficiency in modern industrial ranking systems.

</details>


### [119] [DynamicPO: Dynamic Preference Optimization for Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00327)
*Xingyu Hu,Kai Zhang,Jiancan Wu,Shuli Wang,Chi Wang,Wenshuai Chen,Yinhua Zhu,Haitao Wang,Xingxing Wang,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM推荐系统中的多负样本偏好优化问题，发现并分析了"偏好优化崩溃"现象（增加负样本反而降低性能），提出了DynamicPO框架，通过动态边界负样本选择和双间隔动态β调整来缓解梯度抑制问题，在三个数据集上验证了其有效性且计算开销可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推荐系统中的直接偏好优化(DPO)虽然有效，但存在多负样本优化时的"偏好优化崩溃"问题：训练损失持续下降但性能反而恶化。根本原因是简单负样本压制了边界关键负样本的梯度，导致决策边界模糊。需要解决如何有效利用大量隐式反馈负样本来锐化偏好边界的问题。

Method: 提出DynamicPO轻量级框架：1）动态边界负样本选择机制：识别并优先优化决策边界附近的信息量大的负样本；2）双间隔动态β调整机制：根据边界模糊程度按样本调整优化强度。该框架即插即用，计算开销可忽略。

Result: 在三个公开数据集上的大量实验表明，DynamicPO有效防止了优化崩溃，显著提升了多负样本偏好优化方法的推荐精度，且几乎不增加额外计算负担。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了偏好优化崩溃的梯度抑制机理，提出的DynamicPO框架通过动态选择边界关键负样本和调整优化强度，有效缓解了该问题，为LLM推荐系统的实践提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: In large language model (LLM)-based recommendation systems, direct preference optimization (DPO) effectively aligns recommendations with user preferences, requiring multi-negative objective functions to leverage abundant implicit-feedback negatives and sharpen preference boundaries. However, our empirical analyses reveal a counterintuitive phenomenon, preference optimization collapse, where increasing the number of negative samples can lead to performance degradation despite a continuously decreasing training loss. We further theoretically demonstrate that this collapse arises from gradient suppression, caused by the dominance of easily discriminable negatives over boundary-critical negatives that truly define user preference boundaries. As a result, boundary-relevant signals are under-optimized, weakening the model's decision boundary. Motivated by these observations, we propose DynamicPO (Dynamic Preference Optimization), a lightweight and plug-and-play framework comprising two adaptive mechanisms: Dynamic Boundary Negative Selection, which identifies and prioritizes informative negatives near the model's decision boundary, and Dual-Margin Dynamic beta Adjustment, which calibrates optimization strength per sample according to boundary ambiguity. Extensive experiments on three public datasets show that DynamicPO effectively prevents optimization collapse and improves recommendation accuracy on multi-negative preference optimization methods, with negligible computational overhead. Our code and datasets are available at https://github.com/xingyuHuxingyu/DynamicPO.

</details>


### [120] [Negative Data Mining for Contrastive Learning in Dense Retrieval at IKEA.com](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00353)
*Eva Agapaki,Amritpal Singh Gill*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对宜家产品搜索，本文提出结构化负采样和可扩展LLM评估方法，通过产品层级分类和属性生成语义负样本，并构建LLM打分系统。离线实验提升2.6%类目准确率，但A/B测试显示用户行为无显著改善，因67%搜索为零点击，强调需将训练数据与真实用户行为对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对比学习的效果严重依赖负样本质量，而传统随机采样或稀疏人工标注难以生成语义上具有挑战性的负样本。宜家搜索场景下，需要更系统的方法来提升稠密检索效果，并解决离线评估与在线用户参与度之间的鸿沟。

Method: 基于宜家搜索引擎的后期交互检索架构，提出两大方法：(1) 结构化负采样策略，利用产品层级分类体系和属性信息生成语义难度更高的负样本；(2) 全面的LLM评估方法，为所有候选产品分配相关性分数，替代人工标注。

Result: 在加拿大市场的离线真实用户查询实验中，平均类目准确率提升+2.6%。但针对长尾查询的A/B测试显示，改进模型与基线模型在用户参与度指标上无统计学显著差异(p>0.05)。分析发现67%的热门搜索零点击率超过50%。

Conclusion: 硬负样本挖掘至关重要，但必须将训练数据和离线评估建立在真实用户搜索行为基础上，包括查询意图分布和零点击模式，才能弥合离线检索质量与在线用户参与度之间的差距。仅提升技术指标不足以改善实际用户体验。

Abstract: Contrastive learning is a core component of modern retrieval systems, but its effectiveness heavily relies on the quality of negative examples used during training. In this work, we present a systematic approach to improving dense retrieval for IKEA product search through structured negative sampling strategies and scalable LLM-as-a-judge relevance evaluation.
  Building on IKEA Search Engine's late-interaction retrieval architectures, we introduce two key contributions: (1) structured negative sampling strategies that leverage product hierarchical taxonomy and product attributes to generate semantically challenging negatives, and (2) a comprehensive LLM-based evaluation methodology for generating training data. Rather than relying on sparse human annotations or random sampling, our LLM-based evaluation system allocates a score for all candidate products against each query.
  Our methodology achieves +2.6\% average category accuracy on offline real user query experiments on the Canada market. However, our A/B test on long-tail queries showed no statistically significant differences in user engagement metrics between the improved and baseline models ($p > 0.05$). We trace this gap to user search behavior: 67\% of popular searches exhibit zero-click rates above 50\%, indicating that a substantial proportion of search sessions result in no product engagement regardless of result ranking. These findings underscore the importance of hard negative mining but also the need for grounding training data and offline evals in real user search behavior -- including query intent distribution and zero-click patterns -- to bridge the gap between offline retrieval quality and online user engagement.

### [121] [FollowTable: A Benchmark for Instruction-Following Table Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00400)
*Rihui Jin,Yuchen Lu,Ting Zhang,Jun Wang,Kuicai Dong,Zhaocheng Du,Dongping Liu,Gang Wang,Yong Liu,Guilin Qi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了指令驱动表格检索（IFTR）新任务，以解决传统表格检索仅关注主题相似性而忽略细粒度指令约束的问题。通过构建大规模基准FollowTable和新指标Instruction Responsiveness Score，研究发现现有模型在内容范围和模式约束感知方面存在系统性偏差，表明该领域有重大改进空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM智能体系统的普及，对结构化数据的访问日益需要遵循明确的指令约束，而非仅依赖主题相似性。传统表格检索方法无法满足这种新需求，导致实际应用中相关性判断不准确。因此，需要重新定义表格检索任务，使其能够同时满足主题相关性和细粒度的指令约束。

Method: 形式化定义IFTR任务，构建FollowTable大规模基准数据集（采用分类学驱动的标注流程），并提出Instruction Responsiveness Score评估指标来衡量检索排名相对于纯主题基线的指令适应性。通过系统评估揭示现有模型的缺陷。

Result: 实验结果表明，现有检索模型在IFTR任务上表现不佳：1）对表面语义线索存在系统性偏见；2）难以处理基于模式的约束（如列语义和表示粒度）；3）无法有效满足内容范围要求（如包含与排除约束）。这揭示了当前模型在细粒度指令遵循能力方面的严重不足。

Conclusion: IFTR是一个具有挑战性且重要的新研究方向。当前模型远未达到理想性能，特别是在理解复杂指令和模式约束方面存在明显缺陷。未来的工作需要重点关注提升模型对内容范围、列语义和表示粒度的理解能力，以更好地支持LLM智能体系统对表格数据的指令驱动访问。

Abstract: Table Retrieval (TR) has traditionally been formulated as an ad-hoc retrieval problem, where relevance is primarily determined by topical semantic similarity. With the growing adoption of LLM-based agentic systems, access to structured data is increasingly instruction-driven, where relevance is conditional on explicit content and schema constraints rather than topical similarity alone. We therefore formalize Instruction-Following Table Retrieval (IFTR), a new task that requires models to jointly satisfy topical relevance and fine-grained instruction constraints. We identify two core challenges in IFTR: (i) sensitivity to content scope, such as inclusion and exclusion constraints, and (ii) awareness of schema-grounded requirements, including column semantics and representation granularity--capabilities largely absent in existing retrievers. To support systematic evaluation, we introduce FollowTable, the first large-scale benchmark for IFTR, constructed via a taxonomy-driven annotation pipeline. We further propose a new metric, termed the Instruction Responsiveness Score, to evaluate whether retrieval rankings consistently adapt to user instructions relative to a topic-only baseline. Our results indicate that existing retrieval models struggle to follow fine-grained instructions over tabular data. In particular, they exhibit systematic biases toward surface-level semantic cues and remain limited in handling schema-grounded constraints, highlighting substantial room for future improvements.

### [122] [MUDY: Multi-Granular Dynamic Candidate Contextualization for Unsupervised Keyphrase Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00597)
*Hyeongu Kang,Susik Yoon*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出MUDY框架，通过多粒度上下文显著性来改进关键词抽取，解决了现有预训练语言模型方法在捕捉局部上下文重要性方面的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于预训练语言模型的关键词抽取方法虽然能有效捕获全局语义相关性，但在捕捉与文档中分散子主题相关的关键词局部上下文重要性方面表现不足。

Method: 提出MUDY上下文中心框架，包含两个互补组件：(1)基于提示的评分机制，通过候选词感知加权更好反映局部上下文重要性；(2)基于自注意力的评分机制，利用多粒度注意力模式从文档整体和片段特定层面评估候选关键词重要性。

Result: 在四个真实数据集上的评估表明，MUDY在不同截断阈值下的top-k准确率均优于最先进基线方法。

Conclusion: MUDY框架通过多粒度显著性实现了有效的上下文中心关键词抽取，研究代码已开源。

Abstract: Keyphrase extraction aims to automatically identify concise phrases that effectively represent the content of a document. While recent methods leveraging pre-trained language models (PLMs) have significantly improved the extraction of keyphrases with strong global semantic relevance, they often fall short in capturing the local contextual importance of keyphrases tied to specific subtopics dispersed in a document. In this paper, we propose a novel context-centric framework, MUDY, that effectively captures multi-granular contextual salience of candidate keyphrases. MUDY employs two complementary components: (1) a prompt-based scoring that estimates the generation likelihood of each candidate keyphrase, augmented with candidate-aware weighting to better reflect its local contextual importance, and (2) a self-attention-based scoring that utilizes multi-granular attention patterns from PLMs to assess candidate significance at both the document-wide and segment-specific levels. Evaluations on four real-world datasets demonstrate that MUDY outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in top-k accuracy at various cutoff thresholds. In-depth quantitative and qualitative analyses further highlight the efficacy of context-centric keyphrase extraction with multi-granular saliency. For reproducibility, the source code of MUDY is available at https://github.com/HgKang1/MUDY.

### [123] [A Replicability Study of XTR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00646)
*Rohan Jha,Reno Kriz,Benjamin Van Durme*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本研究复现了XTR检索算法及其修改的训练目标，并扩展到知识蒸馏和高效检索引擎(PLAID/WARP)。虽然验证了token-level匹配特性，但未能在受控比较中复现XTR相对于ColBERT的整体效果优势。关键发现是XTR训练通过 flatten ColBERT的peaked token score分布，提高了centroid scores的区分度，从而在任何使用IVF引擎的部署环境中都带来更高效的检索，而不仅限于原研究的低-k'场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始XTR论文声称需要修改训练目标才能有效进行imputation，且标准ColBERT token scoring不适合imputation。本研究旨在复现并验证这些主张，同时扩展到现代检索引擎设置（知识蒸馏和PLAID/WARP），为实践者提供具体的使用指导。

Method: 复现XTR检索算法及其修改的训练目标；在知识蒸馏(KD)训练和高效检索引擎(PLAID和WARP)上扩展评估；进行受控比较以验证XTR相对于ColBERT的效果优势；分析token score distribution的变化及其对IVF检索效率的影响。

Result: 1) 确认了原始工作声称的token-level匹配特性；2) 在受控比较中未能复现XTR相对于ColBERT的整体效果优势；3) 发现XTR训练通过 flatten ColBERT特有的peaked token score分布，产生更具区分性的centroid scores；4) XTR训练在PLAID和WARP等IVF引擎中带来更高效检索；5) XTR训练的有效性不仅限于低-k'场景，而是扩展到任何IVF-based部署环境。

Conclusion: XTR训练的主要价值在于其机制性影响：通过调整token score分布提升centroid scores的区分度，从而优化IVF检索效率。这一优势适用于广泛的IVF-based部署场景，而不仅限于原始研究的特定条件，为实践者提供了更清晰的XTR使用指南。

Abstract: The XTR (conteXtual Token Retrieval) algorithm is a modification to ColBERT retrieval that avoids the costly step of fully gathering and reranking the candidates' embeddings by imputing their missing similarity scores from the initial token retrieval step. The original work proposes a modified training objective as necessary for effective XTR retrieval, arguing that standard ColBERT token scoring is unsuitable for imputation. In this paper, we replicate both the XTR retrieval algorithm and its modified training objective, and extend the evaluation to knowledge-distillation (KD) training and efficient retrieval engines (PLAID and WARP). We confirm the token-level matching characteristics claimed in the original work, but fail to replicate XTR's overall effectiveness advantage over ColBERT under a controlled comparison. We further show that XTR's training modification has a concrete mechanistic consequence for modern retrieval engines: by flattening ColBERT's characteristically peaked token score distribution, XTR training yields more discriminative centroid scores and thus more efficient IVF-based retrieval under PLAID and WARP. The utility of XTR training is therefore not limited to the low-$k'$ regime originally studied, but extends to any deployment setting where IVF-based engines are used. These findings offer practitioners concrete guidance on how and when to use XTR as their multi-vector retriever.

### [124] [Robust Multimodal Recommendation via Graph Retrieval-Enhanced Modality Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00670)
*Yuan Li,Jun Hu,Jiaxin Jiang,Bryan Hooi,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对多模态推荐中因传感器故障、标注稀缺或隐私约束导致的模态缺失问题，本文提出GRE-MC框架，通过模态感知子图检索与图transformer联合编码实现缺失模态补全，在基准测试中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际Web推荐系统中的多模态数据常因传感器故障、标注成本高昂或隐私保护限制而出现模态缺失，严重降低模型可靠性。传统补全方法仅利用节点自身或邻域信息，难以捕获图结构中隐含的丰富语义上下文。

Method: 提出图检索增强的模态补全框架GRE-MC，核心包括：1) 模态感知子图检索机制，从全图中筛选语义相关子图以获取丰富上下文；2) 基于全局注意力的图transformer，联合编码查询节点与检索子图以补全缺失特征；3) 可学习稀疏路由码本，将潜在嵌入正则化为紧凑基以提升鲁棒性。

Result: 在多模态推荐基准数据集上的大量实验验证，GRE-MC在各项指标上持续超越现有最先进方法，证明了所提组件的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作证实了子图检索与联合编码图transformer在模态补全任务中的关键作用，为构建鲁棒的多模态推荐系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Multimodal data plays a critical role in web-based recommendation systems, where information from diverse modalities such as vision and text enhances representation learning. However, real-world multimodal datasets often suffer from modality incompleteness due to sensor failures, annotation scarcity, or privacy constraints, which substantially degrade model performance and reliability. One effective solution to address this issue is modality completion, which reconstructs missing features to provide modality-complete graphs for downstream tasks. Given a query node with missing multimodal features, existing modality completion methods typically infer information from the node itself or its neighbors to reconstruct the missing modality. However, these methods may overlook semantically relevant context in the graph, which contains valuable cues that are non-trivial to capture through simple methods like neighborhood aggregation. In this work, we propose GRE-MC, a Graph Retrieval-Enhanced Modality Completion framework, to overcome these limitations. By introducing a modality-aware subgraph retrieval mechanism, GRE-MC selects semantically relevant subgraphs from the entire graph, providing richer contextual information for completing missing modalities. Subsequently, a graph transformer jointly encodes the query node and the retrieved subgraph via global attention to complete the missing features, while a learnable sparse-routing codebook regularizes latent embeddings into compact bases for improved robustness. Extensive experiments on multimodal recommendation benchmarks demonstrate that GRE-MC consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, validating the effectiveness of subgraph retrieval and joint-encoding graph transformer for robust modality completion.

</details>
